                <h1>Research and enterprise</h1>
            <p class="lead">ACU develops innovative solutions to issues impacting human dignity and the common good. Our interdisciplinary and collaborative research seeks to enable people to develop intellectually, spiritually, physically, socially, and emotionally, to enable flourishing lives, foster thriving communities and build an ethical future.</p>

            <div class="row">
                <div class="col-md-12 desktop-width slider margin-bottom--2-5">
                    <h2>Our research</h2>
                        <p></p>

                </div>

            </div>

            <div id="slider472">
                <!--filters-->
                <!--main carousel element-->
                    <div class="owl-carousel content_carousel">
                                <div class="project  slider-container">
                                        <a href="https://impact.acu.edu.au/study/seeing-the-law-through-an-indigenous-lens" data-track-category="carousel" data-track-action="call to action" data-track-label="Seeing the law through an Indigenous lens" target="" class="as-block has-type-tag">
                                           
                                            <img src="/-/media/feature/carousel/2024/a5084_seeing-the-law-through-an-indigenous-lens_main-image1.jpg?h=340&amp;w=300&amp;la=en&amp;hash=C7A888715A84BC50816E3E32FBA8D960" class="as-block slide" alt=" " />
                                            <h3 class="subhead">Seeing the law through an Indigenous lens</h3>
                                            <small></small>
                                            <p>In the early 1970s, when Mick Dodson was on his way to becoming the first Aboriginal man to graduate with a law degree, Indigenous issues barely got a mention in the curriculum. This was a time of great activism and change, with Aboriginal legal services being established all over the country, and the powerful land rights movement gaining pace.</p>
                                        </a>
                                </div>
                                <div class="project  slider-container">
                                        <a href="https://impact.acu.edu.au/lifestyle/call-for-calm-on-screen-time-concerns" data-track-category="carousel" data-track-action="call to action" data-track-label="Call for calm on screen time concerns" target="" class="as-block has-type-tag">
                                           
                                            <img src="/-/media/feature/carousel/2024/ic5077_call-for-calm-on-screen-time-concerns_main-image.jpg?h=340&amp;w=300&amp;la=en&amp;hash=6E0FA897E226486BB019F9AF41209CEF" class="as-block slide" alt=" " />
                                            <h3 class="subhead">Call for calm on screen time concerns</h3>
                                            <small></small>
                                            <p>The much-celebrated Swiss physician and naturalist, Conrad Gessner, was well known for his dramatic declaration that a ubiquitous new technology would be "confusing and harmful" to the human mind, thereby leading society into ruin. And Gessner wasn't the first to warn of the dangers posed by this innovation. Others, like the Italian writer Filippo de Strata, asserted it would "corrupt susceptible hearts". So, which harmful invention were these scholars railing against?</p>
                                        </a>
                                </div>
                                <div class="project  slider-container">
                                        <a href="https://impact.acu.edu.au/lifestyle/multitasking-in-a-wired-world" data-track-category="carousel" data-track-action="call to action" data-track-label="Multitasking in a wired world" target="" class="as-block has-type-tag">
                                           
                                            <img src="/-/media/feature/carousel/2024/s5067_multitasking-in-a-wired-world_main-image.jpg?h=340&amp;w=300&amp;la=en&amp;hash=7C3550E68FCF2F91FE7B42BBA001A81D" class="as-block slide" alt=" " />
                                            <h3 class="subhead">Multitasking in a wired world</h3>
                                            <small></small>
                                            <p>It's no secret that when trying to focus on more than one tricky task at a time, performance tends to suffer. The most skilled of chefs will find it harder to avoid spills and burns if they're talking on the phone to a debt collector at the same time. The most astute of managers might struggle to chair a meeting if they're also scanning their device for news on an ill relative.</p>
                                        </a>
                                </div>
                                <div class="project  slider-container">
                                        <a href="https://impact.acu.edu.au/lifestyle/combining-clinical-care-with-cutting-edge-research" data-track-category="carousel" data-track-action="call to action" data-track-label="Combining clinical care with cutting-edge research" target="" class="as-block has-type-tag">
                                           
                                            <img src="/-/media/feature/carousel/2024/ic5057_combining-clinical-care-with-cutting-edge-research_main-image.jpg?h=340&amp;w=300&amp;la=en&amp;hash=69BFF511327648AA79521243CDBD581A" class="as-block slide" alt=" " />
                                            <h3 class="subhead">Combining clinical care with cutting-edge research</h3>
                                            <small></small>
                                            <p>When it comes to injuries, a torn anterior cruciate ligament (ACL) is among the greatest of fears for athletes. Often requiring reconstructive surgery and many months of rehabilitation, this common knee injury can be life changing.</p>
                                        </a>
                                </div>
                                <div class="project  slider-container">
                                        <a href="https://impact.acu.edu.au/community/wading-through-a-web-of-information" data-track-category="carousel" data-track-action="call to action" data-track-label="Wading through a web of information" target="" class="as-block has-type-tag">
                                           
                                            <img src="/-/media/feature/carousel/2024/ic5059_wading-through-a-web-of-information_main-image.jpg?h=340&amp;w=300&amp;la=en&amp;hash=473E071E07D414C027CE9F60651EFE33" class="as-block slide" alt=" " />
                                            <h3 class="subhead">Wading through a web of information</h3>
                                            <small></small>
                                            <p>A close friend approaches to tell you they're concerned about the health risks of using their mobile phone. You're a trusted mate, and they're keen to hear your opinion about the safety of their device. "I'm no expert," you say to your friend, "but let me do some research and get back to you."</p>
                                        </a>
                                </div>
                                <div class="project  slider-container">
                                        <a href="https://impact.acu.edu.au/global/how-struggling-readers-become-anxious-kids" data-track-category="carousel" data-track-action="call to action" data-track-label="How struggling readers become anxious kids" target="" class="as-block has-type-tag">
                                           
                                            <img src="/-/media/feature/carousel/2024/ic5062_how-struggling-readers-become-anxious-kids_main-image.jpg?h=340&amp;w=300&amp;la=en&amp;hash=7B03754E0A3AFA2A7797AC09AB580AED" class="as-block slide" alt=" " />
                                            <h3 class="subhead">How struggling readers become anxious kids</h3>
                                            <small></small>
                                            <p>Over a decade ago, literacy expert Genevieve McArthur took a phone call from a distressed mother whose son was not only struggling with reading at school, his emotional health had also begun to spiral.
